<p>America is a nation at war; at war with itself. This isn't a fault in the system — it is an inherent feature of its design.</p>

        </span><span class="hl-reserved">margin-top:</span><span class="hl-code"> </span><span class="hl-number">0.15</span><span class="hl-code">rem</span><span class="hl-code">;
    </span><span class="hl-brackets">}</span><span class="hl-code">
 
    </span><span class="hl-identifier">#top-bar</span><span class="hl-code">,
    </span><span class="hl-identifier">#top-bar</span><span class="hl-code"> </span><span class="hl-identifier">a</span><span class="hl-code"> </span><span class="hl-brackets">{</span><span class="hl-code">
        </span><span class="hl-reserved">top:</span><span class="hl-code"> </span><span class="hl-number">8.3</span><span class="hl-code">rem</span><span class="hl-code">;
        </span><span class="hl-reserved">font-size:</span><span class="hl-code"> </span><span class="hl-number">90</span><span class="hl-string">%</span><span class="hl-code">;
    </span><span class="hl-brackets">}</span><span class="hl-code">
 
    </span><span class="hl-identifier">div#header</span><span class="hl-code"> </span><span class="hl-brackets">{</span><span class="hl-code">
        </span><span class="hl-reserved">height:</span><span class="hl-code"> </span><span class="hl-number">123</span><span class="hl-string">px</span><span class="hl-code">;
    </span><span class="hl-brackets">}</span><span class="hl-code">
 
}
 
</span><span class="hl-var">@media</span><span class="hl-code"> (max-width: 520</span><span class="hl-identifier">px</span><span class="hl-code">) </span><span class="hl-brackets">{</span><span class="hl-code">
 
    </span><span class="hl-identifier">#header</span><span class="hl-code"> </span><span class="hl-reserved">h2:</span><span class="hl-code">:before {
        line-height: </span><span class="hl-number">16</span><span class="hl-string">px</span><span class="hl-code">;
        </span><span class="hl-reserved">margin-top:</span><span class="hl-code"> </span><span class="hl-number">0.5</span><span class="hl-code">rem</span><span class="hl-code">;
    </span><span class="hl-brackets">}</span><span class="hl-code">
 
    </span><span class="hl-identifier">#top-bar</span><span class="hl-code">,
    </span><span class="hl-identifier">#top-bar</span><span class="hl-code"> </span><span class="hl-identifier">a</span><span class="hl-code"> </span><span class="hl-brackets">{</span><span class="hl-code">
        </span><span class="hl-reserved">top:</span><span class="hl-code"> </span><span class="hl-number">9.3</span><span class="hl-code">rem</span><span class="hl-code">;
    </span><span class="hl-brackets">}</span><span class="hl-code">
 
    </span><span class="hl-identifier">div#header</span><span class="hl-code"> </span><span class="hl-brackets">{</span><span class="hl-code">
        </span><span class="hl-reserved">height:</span><span class="hl-code"> </span><span class="hl-number">145</span><span class="hl-string">px</span><span class="hl-code">;
    </span><span class="hl-brackets">}</span><span class="hl-code">
 
}</span></pre></div>

<p><span style="white-space: pre-wrap;"> </span></p>
<div class="president">
<p>[…] America is a nation at war. At war with malicious, foreign influence.</p>
<p>From every corner of the globe, you will all hear from groups focused on destabilizing the western world. You will hear how the situation is the fault of our country — how it is <span style="text-decoration: underline;">we</span> who released the virus worldwide, threatening our shared occult legacy.</p>
<p>I implore you all to consider who you hear those words from. Is it from the warmongers of the Global Occult Coalition, who will stop at nothing to push their globalist agenda against the interests of America? Or is it from the far-left radicals, international and domestic, whose ranks are full of dangerous magical criminals who threaten the very values that this country was built upon?</p>
<p>In spite of these lies, remember this: we are the ones who will bring you and your family the stability Americans deserve. We are not cowards — we do not hesitate when duty calls us. We do not tread on the same ground as our predecessors, hesitant to react to crises all over the world. We answer when our country cries out for help.</p>
<p>God bless America, for with us she will endure. […]</p>
<p><em>Daniel Reed Crenshaw</em><br>
<em>52nd President of the United States of America</em></p>
</div>
<p><span style="white-space: pre-wrap;"> </span></p>
<div class="al-fine">
<p>[…] The Washington Virion is the single biggest threat to humanity since the Impasse.</p>
<p>I have been approached many times by people from every end of the political spectrum, all asking if I truly believe that declaring Procedure Pizzicato on the USA was justified; whether declaring martial law on a sovereign country is something to be proud of. And every time I hear the same words, citing our interventionism as somehow threatening the safety of American citizens.</p>
<p>Let me tell you this: Pizzicato is the <span style="text-decoration: underline;">only</span> way to ensure humanity's survival. As the Global Occult Coalition, we will protect the shared legacy of mankind that we have all built, regardless of whether it conflicts with the interests of a singular nation. We will fight KTE-9817 with an iron fist, no matter the consequences — for when faced with the threat of extinguishing the flame of humanity, there is no middle ground. […]</p>
<p><em>Undersecretary General D.C. al Fine</em><br>
<em>United Nations Global Occult Coalition</em></p>
</div>
<p><span style="white-space: pre-wrap;"> </span></p>
<div class="vanguard">
<p>[…] To this extent, Vanguard will do anything in its might to help the victims of the virus. But we are not almighty.</p>
<p>Truth be told, the situation is a mess — one we cannot possibly hope to untangle alone. Between the Coalition, Phoenix Technologies, and the US Government, the playing field is more akin to a minefield. But we can navigate it safely together, of that I'm certain. The clock is ticking, but we <span style="text-decoration: underline;">will</span> succeed — because united, there is nothing we cannot do. There is no task too great for us, I guarantee you that.</p>
<p>Have faith, friends. That's the least you can do. […]</p>
<p><em>Dr. Jay Everwood</em><br>
<em>Director of the Vanguard Department of External Affairs</em></p>
</div>
<p><span style="white-space: pre-wrap;"> </span><br>
<span style="white-space: pre-wrap;"> </span><br>
<span style="white-space: pre-wrap;"> </span></p>
<div class="blockquote">
<div class="image-container aligncenter"><img src="https://scp-wiki.wdfiles.com/local--files/kte-9817-bluebuster-mendel-shelley-renegade-armbrusteri/wpho.png" height="100px" alt="wpho.png" class="image"></div>

<div style="text-align: center;">
<h1 id="toc23"><span>Information Overview</span></h1>
</div>
<hr>
<ul>
<li><strong>What is this?</strong></li>
</ul>
<p>8,000 Dead Rats is an open series that explores the global aftermath of the US Government creating and inadvertently releasing a virus aimed at controlling the American population of magically-gifted individuals. As the USA is quarantined off from the rest of the world to halt the spread of the virus, the magic legacy of the whole world is once again at stake for the first time in almost three decades. With parties from all over the globe coming in to deal with the situation in tens of unique ways, the series asks what would realistically occur should the wonder of the new, Veilless world of the near future be fatally threatened.</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Who can contribute?</strong></li>
</ul>
<p>Anyone! 8,000 Dead Rats is an open series, meaning anyone and everyone is more than welcome to add to any of its arcs. We actively invite anyone interested to contribute — there are tons of unique opportunities and angles to show the global event from, so we would love to see how your particular corner of the SCP world would react to the pandemic.</p>
<p>However, we highly recommend reading already existing articles in the series prior to contributing, as the series aims to remain internally consistent and coherent between its events, ensuring that it does not contradict itself. There aren't any real rules to contributing, aside from respecting the works of others and operating within the confines of the From 120's Archives canon. If you're unsure how parts of this world operate, make sure to check out the canon's hub or ask around in the discussion of the series' articles.</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>I'm interested. Where can I talk with other contributors?</strong></li>
</ul>
<p>Discussions related to 8,000 Dead Rats regularly happen in the #from-120s-archives channel on the CANONEXUS Discord server (<a href="https://discord.gg/34hnt4jeMT">invite link</a>), where most of its contributors hang out and where coordinating further developments to the series happens. If you want to contribute to the series or simply want to chat — feel free to pop in! Alternatively, if Discord isn't really your thing, please don't be afraid to reach out to <span class="printuser avatarhover"><a href="http://www.wikidot.com/user:info/jasiu06" onclick="WIKIDOT.page.listeners.userInfo(6669398); return false;"><img class="small" src="https://www.wikidot.com/avatar.php?userid=6669398&amp;amp;size=small&amp;amp;timestamp=1776161599" alt="Jasiu06" style="background-image:url(https://www.wikidot.com/userkarma.php?u=6669398)"></a><a href="http://www.wikidot.com/user:info/jasiu06" onclick="WIKIDOT.page.listeners.userInfo(6669398); return false;">Jasiu06</a></span> or <span class="printuser avatarhover"><a href="http://www.wikidot.com/user:info/ralliston" onclick="WIKIDOT.page.listeners.userInfo(5986843); return false;"><img class="small" src="https://www.wikidot.com/avatar.php?userid=5986843&amp;amp;size=small&amp;amp;timestamp=1776161599" alt="Ralliston" style="background-image:url(https://www.wikidot.com/userkarma.php?u=5986843)"></a><a href="http://www.wikidot.com/user:info/ralliston" onclick="WIKIDOT.page.listeners.userInfo(5986843); return false;">Ralliston</a></span> if you have any further inquiries.</p>
</div>
<div id="wiki-tab-0-1" style="display:none">
<div style="text-align: center;">
<h1 id="toc24"><span>Active Players</span></h1>
</div>
<hr>
<div class="characters">
<div class="characters-top">
<div class="goc bar"></div>
<div class="characters-info">
<p><strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;">NAME:</span></strong> D.C. al Fine<br>
<strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;">GENDER:</span></strong> <tt>[CLASSIFIED]</tt><br>
<strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;">TITLE:</span></strong> Undersecretary General of the Global Occult Coalition</p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="bio">
<p><strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;">BRIEFING:</span></strong> Veteran battlemage acting as the Undersecretary General of the Global Occult Coalition. Leads the Coalition's attempts at containing the virus with an iron fist, tolerating no resistance against her geopolitical campaign. Though appears to hold good intentions, pursues her own agendas in the wake of the pandemic. Considers PENTAGRAM — and, by extension, all of the Crenshaw Administration — a minor obstacle that nevertheless opposes the interests of humanity and the Coalition. Firm believer of Coalition interventionism.</p>
</div>
</div>
<hr>
<div class="characters">
<div class="characters-top">
<div class="joicl bar"></div>
<div class="characters-info">
<p><strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;">NAME:</span></strong> Haru Yoshida<br>
<strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;">GENDER:</span></strong> Male<br>
<strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;">TITLE:</span></strong> Professor of Science; JOICL Virology Division Director</p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="bio">
<p><strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;">BRIEFING:</span></strong> Talented JOICL scientist specializing in virology. Hired by his mentor and Humanoid Organism Laboratory Director, Hisashi Kunō, in 2028 after graduating from ICSUT Tokyo. Close collaborator of the US Government and PENTAGRAM; the mastermind behind the team that artificially developed the virus. With a weak moral compass — will take on any project for the self-perceived interests of science and his own monetary gain. Does not consider himself to be in any way at fault for the current situation, putting the blame solely on the reckless Crenshaw Administration.</p>
</div>
</div>
<hr>
<div class="characters">
<div class="characters-top">
<div class="mcd bar"></div>
<div class="characters-info">
<p><strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;">NAME:</span></strong> Robert Carter<br>
<strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;">GENDER:</span></strong> Male<br>
<strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;">TITLE:</span></strong> Senior Partner of Marshall, Carter &amp; Dark</p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="bio">
<p><strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;">BRIEFING:</span></strong> Narcissistic trillionaire and one of the three leaders of the Marshall, Carter &amp; Dark megacorporation. Without a shred of sympathy for the victims of the virus and other (especially impoverished) people in general; sees the current situation as a fantastic occasion to enrich himself even further. One of the primary minds behind the Carter Courier Channel, a transport network aimed at maintaining global trade in and out of the United States in spite of its quarantine.</p>
</div>
</div>
<hr>
<div class="characters">
<div class="characters-top">
<div class="phoenix bar"></div>
<div class="characters-info">
<p><strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;">NAME:</span></strong> Simón Torres<br>
<strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;">GENDER:</span></strong> Male<br>
<strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;">TITLE:</span></strong> CEO of Phoenix Technologies</p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="bio">
<p><strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;">BRIEFING:</span></strong> CEO of Phoenix Technologies and leader of the Coalition-anointed joint research team. Self-serving and egocentric, though a brilliant parascientist; extremely intelligent, and highly resourceful. Aids the research effort focused on developing a cure to the virus with all his might, but sees the situation mostly as an opportunity to further his own goals and gain splendor for himself and his company.</p>
</div>
</div>
<hr>
<div class="characters">
<div class="characters-top">
<div class="us bar"></div>
<div class="characters-info">
<p><strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;">NAME:</span></strong> Thomas Bowe<br>
<strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;">GENDER:</span></strong> Male<br>
<strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;">TITLE:</span></strong> US Army General; Senior Extraordinary Resources Advisor</p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="bio">
<p><strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;">BRIEFING:</span></strong> United States Army General and one of the most prominent members of PENTAGRAM. Grandson of Stanley Bowe and nephew of the infamous <a href="/resurrection-old-foes-hub">George Bowe</a>; bears his position due to years of nepotism inside the US Military. A conservative relic of a bygone era; as a collaborator of Haru Yoshida and the primary liaison in PENTAGRAM projects related to the virus, bears little empathy or concern for others, particularly minorities. Possesses questionable morals stemming from a life rooted in military service. Attempts to alleviate Coalition control over his country and save PENTAGRAM's reputation, though with questionable results.</p>
</div>
</div>
<hr>
<div class="characters">
<div class="characters-top">
<div class="us bar"></div>
<div class="characters-info">
<p><strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;">NAME:</span></strong> Daniel Crenshaw<br>
<strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;">GENDER:</span></strong> Male<br>
<strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;">TITLE:</span></strong> President of the United States</p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="bio">
<p><strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;">BRIEFING:</span></strong> The 52nd President of the United States of America and former Navy SEAL; a firm Republican. Reckless, bigoted, and deeply conservative — believes that commissioning the creation of the virus, though catastrophic in consequences, was justified as means of combatting questionably existent social issues. Sees no fault of his own in the current situation. Initially attempted to trick the Coalition into handling the virus for him, but deeply underestimated who he was dealing with; deeply opposes the Coalition's attempts at taking control of his country.</p>
</div>
</div>
<hr>
<div class="characters">
<div class="characters-top">
<div class="us bar"></div>
<div class="characters-info">
<p><strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;">NAME:</span></strong> Thomas Graham<br>
<strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;">GENDER:</span></strong> Male<br>
<strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;">TITLE:</span></strong> United States Secretary of State</p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="bio">
<p><strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;">BRIEFING:</span></strong> Former Site-17 Director under the late SCP Foundation. Noted for his cruelty and lack of ethics even by former standards; kept his position due to his high efficiency. Prosecuted in a high-stakes trial following the collapse of the Veil, and ultimately pardoned by President Crenshaw. Highly driven by and obsessed with the idea of bringing back the "good old days" of Foundation-enforced Normalcy. Disgusted by anything paranormal; privately celebrates the spread of the virus. Despised by the public, particularly by members of Vanguard who remember working with him.</p>
</div>
</div>
<hr>
<div class="characters">
<div class="characters-top">
<div class="van bar"></div>
<div class="characters-info">
<p><strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;">NAME:</span></strong> Jay Everwood<br>
<strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;">GENDER:</span></strong> Non-binary<br>
<strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;">TITLE:</span></strong> Vanguard External Affairs Director</p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="bio">
<p><strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;">BRIEFING:</span></strong> Head of Vanguard's diplomatic arm and de-facto leader of its inter-organizational communication. Liaison of the group's collaboration efforts and the front face of its campaign against the virus. Firm believer in cooperation aimed at stopping the virus; with a genuine intent to save as many people as they possibly can.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div id="wiki-tab-0-2" style="display:none">
<div style="text-align: center;">
<h1 id="toc25"><span>Timeline of Relevant Events</span></h1>
</div>
<hr>
<ul>
<li><strong>2040</strong>
<ul>
<li>Following a bloody months-long insurrection and months more of international scandal, Silesia gains independance as a sovereign republic, separate from Poland. [<a href="/independent-republic-of-silesia">Referenced</a>]</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<ul>
<li><strong>2044</strong>
<ul>
<li>Dan Crenshaw wins the US presidential election. [<a href="/project-scarlet-dawn">Referenced</a>] [<a href="/how-did-we-get-here">Referenced</a>]</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<ul>
<li><strong>2045</strong>
<ul>
<li>Thomas Graham is pardoned by President Crenshaw, allowing for his official entrance onto the scene of US politics. [<a href="/chronicle-of-the-worm">Depicted</a>]</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<ul>
<li><strong>2048</strong>
<ul>
<li>The newly convened 19th National Commission of the Chinese People's Political Consultative Conference introduces radical political, social, and economic reforms to the whole of China's government system.</li>
<li>The United States Paranatural Warfare Command commissions JOICL to create an anti-thaumaturgic virus for political reasons. [<a href="/project-scarlet-dawn">Depicted</a>]</li>
<li><strong>5th of November</strong> — Dan Crenshaw wins the US presidential election for a second time, inadvertently spreading the anti-thaumic virus into Washington, D.C. moments before his inauguration. [<a href="/project-scarlet-dawn">Depicted</a>]</li>
<li><strong>17th of December</strong> — In hopes of halting the further spread of the anti-thaumic virus, the US government authorizes the Global Occult Coalition to intervene and occupy Washington, D.C. The parathreat is designated as KTE-9817-Bluebuster-Mendel-Shelley-Renegade-Armbrusteri and named the Washington Virion. [<a href="/kte-9817-bluebuster-mendel-shelley-renegade-armbrusteri">Depicted</a>]</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<ul>
<li><strong>2049</strong>
<ul>
<li><strong>16th of February</strong> — In a desperate attempt at preventing the spread of the Washington Virion worldwide, the United States of America is officially declared quarantined from the rest of the world by Global Occult Coalition officials. [<a href="/kte-9817-bluebuster-mendel-shelley-renegade-armbrusteri">Depicted</a>]</li>
<li><strong>February</strong> — A Sons of Phomet intervention inside Druv'tuul leads to further conflict between religious fundamentalists, the city's new post-revolution government, and the Chaos Insurgency. [<a href="/sc-049-100-049-103">Depicted</a>]</li>
<li><strong>1st of March</strong> — Following a summit of the world's brightest parascientific minds, the Global Occult Coalition enacts a limited version of Procedure Pizzicato inside the borders of the United States of America. To develop a cure against the Washington Virion, the Coalition forms together a joint team consisting of several parascientific organizations, led by Simón Torres of Phoenix Technologies. [<a href="/arco">Depicted</a>] [<a href="/carter-courier-channel">Referenced</a>]</li>
<li><strong>5th of March</strong> — JOICL releases its Anima Back-Ups product to the public market. [<a href="/joicl8kdr">Depicted</a>]</li>
<li><strong>20th of March</strong> — Vanguard staff refuse the Coalition's demand for the abuse of VNP-8002 for the Coalition's own gain. [<a href="/vnp-8002">Depicted</a>]</li>
<li><strong>4th of May</strong> — Due to complications related to the Washington Virion, Phillip Willis dies. [<a href="/echoes">Referenced</a>]</li>
<li><strong>September</strong> — The impeachment of President Dan Crenshaw fails by a single vote. [<a href="/scientia-potentia-est">Referenced</a>]</li>
<li><strong>October</strong> — As the Phoenix Technologies-led research team produces a cure and vaccine to the Washington Virion, its distribution slowly begins worldwide. [<a href="/scientia-potentia-est">Depicted</a>] [<a href="/wayward-forlorn-kin">Referenced</a>]</li>
<li><strong>December</strong> — The Hadfield twins embark on a journey across the USA to meet with Aaron Siegel and Ranyue Lin. [<a href="/wayward-forlorn-kin">Depicted</a>]</li>
<li><strong>11th of December</strong> — A hearing before the US Senate, held to investigate the case of the Washington Virion, leads to the arrest of General Bowe and the trial of Haru Yoshida. [<a href="/coda-for-the-capitol">Depicted</a>]</li>
<li><strong>11th of December</strong> — During his escape from the country in an attempt to evade the law, US Secretary of State Thomas Graham is assassinated by a Serpent's Hand member. [<a href="/coda-for-the-capitol">Depicted</a>]</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<ul>
<li><strong>2050</strong>
<ul>
<li><strong>January</strong> — Global Occult Coalition forces begin their withdrawal from the USA. [<a href="/coda-for-the-capitol">Depicted</a>]</li>
<li><strong>25th of March</strong> — Jacob Wilson fails to assassinate Dan Crenshaw with a homemade thaumic bomb, leaving the President badly injured and scarred for life, but capable of performing his administrative duties. [<a href="/failed-president-crenshaw-assassination-attempt">Referenced</a>]</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<ul>
<li><strong>2056</strong>
<ul>
<li>Dr. Small receives the Nobel Prize for developing the Asclepius vaccine. [<a href="/scientia-potentia-est">Depicted</a>]</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</div>
</div>
</div>

<h1 id="toc27"><span><span style="font-size:75%;"><tt><em><span style="color: #5e5e5e">The only way to deal with an unfree world is to become so absolutely free that your very existence is an act of rebellion.</span></em></tt></span></span></h1>
<h3 id="toc28"><span><span style="font-size:120%;"><span style="color: #5e5e5e">Albert Camus</span></span></span></h3>
